d_knights_templar = { # Knights Templar
	color = { 230 230 230 }
	color2 = { 255 255 255 }
	graphical_culture = holygfx
	capital = 138 # Orléans # Orleans
	# Always exists
	landless = yes
	holy_order = yes
	mercenary_type = knights_templar_composition
	culture = frankish
	# Parent Religion
	religion = catholic
	# Cannot be held as a secondary title
	primary = yes
	# Extra income due to banking, etc
	monthly_income = 10 # (Must be an integer between 1 and 512)
	title = GRANDMASTER
	title_female = GRANDMASTER
	foa = GRANDMASTER_FOA
}

d_sunni_cuman_company = { # Khazar Company
	color = { 134 155 30 }
	color2 = { 255 255 255 }
	capital = 895 # Yaik
	# Parent Religion
	religion = sunni
	culture = cuman
	mercenary = yes
	# Always exists
	landless = yes
	# Cannot be held as a secondary title
	primary = yes
	# Cannot be vassalized
	independent = yes
	strength_growth_per_century = 1.0
	mercenary_type = muslim_cuman_company_composition
	# Hire Trigger
	allow = {
		conditional_tooltip = {
			trigger = { is_alternate_start = no }

				religion_group = muslim
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			}
		}
	}
	title = CAPTAIN

	foa = CAPTAIN_FOA
}

		}

	}

	allow = {
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { e_roman_empire = { has_holder = yes } }
			e_roman_empire = { has_holder = no }
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { e_latin_empire = { has_holder = yes } }
			e_latin_empire = { has_holder = no }
		}
		c_byzantion = {
			owner_under_ROOT = yes
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { NOT = { empire = { title = FROM } } }
				empire = { title = FROM }
			}
		}
		title_emperor_basic_allow = yes
	}
} # end e_byzantium

			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { is_de_jure_title = no } }
				custom_tooltip = { text = ENGLAND_BECOMES_DE_JURE_TT }
			}
		}
		allow = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { FROM = { is_de_jure_title = no } }
				independent = yes
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CONTROLS_HALF_OF_ENGLISH_REGION_TT
					# AI creates this title solely via explicit maintenance,
					# so none of this is for them
					ai = no
					any_realm_province = {
						# there are 43 counties in the current custom_england;
						# this is >50%
						count = 22
						region = custom_england
					}
				}
			}
			title_king_basic_allow = yes
		}

		gain_effect = {
			# If title receiver also owns the titular Tara, then
			# we can safely destroy and deactivate that title now.
			k_ireland_titular = { # Tara
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_holder = no
							holder = PREV
						}
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						# If it somehow became non-titular, then we must be sure
						# to transfer its de jure territory to k_ireland first.
						any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = { de_jure_liege = k_ireland }
					}
					activate_title = {
						title = THIS
						status = no
					}
					destroy_landed_title = THIS
				}
			}
		}
		allow = { title_king_basic_allow = yes }
	} # end k_ireland

	gain_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				k_naples = { is_de_jure_title = yes }
				NOT = { de_jure_liege = FROM }
			}
			k_naples = {
				show_scope_change = no
				de_jure_liege = FROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				k_trinacria = { is_de_jure_title = yes }
				NOT = { de_jure_liege = FROM }
			}
			k_trinacria = {
				show_scope_change = no
				de_jure_liege = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { religion_group = christian } }
			FROM = { is_de_jure_title = yes }
		}
		has_landed_title = k_italy
		has_landed_title = k_sicily
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				k_naples = { is_de_jure_title = yes }
				NOT = { de_jure_liege = FROM }
			}
			has_landed_title = k_naples
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				k_trinacria = { is_de_jure_title = yes }
				NOT = { de_jure_liege = FROM }
			}
			has_landed_title = k_trinacria
		}
		title_emperor_basic_allow = yes
	}
} # end e_italy

	allow = {
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EMF
				FROM = { has_holder = yes } # Usurpation
			}
			OR = {
				realm_size >= 220
				FROM = { has_law = crown_authority_4 }
			}
		}
		trigger_else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EMF
				FROM = { has_holder = no } # Creation
			}
			OR = {
				realm_size >= 220
				primary_title = {
					OR = {
						has_law = crown_authority_3
						has_law = crown_authority_4
					}
				}
			}
		}
		title_emperor_basic_allow = yes
	}
} # end e_persia

		gain_effect = {
			# If title receiver also owns the titular Hayk, then
			# we can safely destroy and deactivate that title now.
			k_bagratid_grand_principality = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_holder = no
							holder = PREV
						}
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						# If it somehow became non-titular, then we must be sure
						# to transfer its de jure territory to k_armenia first.
						any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = { de_jure_liege = k_armenia }
					}
					activate_title = {
						title = THIS
						status = no
					}
					destroy_landed_title = THIS
				}
			}
		}
		allow = { title_king_basic_allow = yes }
	} # end k_armenia

			religion = catholic
			is_heresy_of = catholic

		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { e_roman_empire = { has_holder = yes } }
			e_roman_empire = { has_holder = no }
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { e_byzantium = { has_holder = yes } }
			e_byzantium = { has_holder = no }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = controls_kaliopolis_thrake
			hidden_tooltip = {
				495 = { # Kaliopolis
					owner_under_ROOT = yes
				}
				497 = { # Thrake
					owner_under_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
		}
		c_byzantion = { owner_under_ROOT = yes }
		title_emperor_basic_allow = yes
	}

		NOT = { has_global_flag = EMF } # EMF+SWMH has special code for a Fourth Crusade-like scenario
		conditional_tooltip = {
			trigger = { e_nicaea = { is_titular = yes } }
			e_nicaea = { is_titular = no }
		}
	}
}
